[30;1m2 | [0m[35m============[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35m- ``save()``:[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35m    Saves the entire state of the canvas.[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35m- ``restore()``:[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35m    Restores the most recently saved canvas state.[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m9 | [0m[35mCanvas states are stored on a stack. Every time the ``save()`` method is called, the current drawing[0m
[30;1m10 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m11 | [0m[35m- The transformations that have been applied (i.e. translate, rotate and scale – see next section).[0m
